settings.RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: Maximum number of requests allowed (default: 100)\n    - settings.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: Time window in seconds (default: 3600)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        # Get configuration from settings with defaults\n        rate_limit_requests = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS\", 100)\n        rate_limit_window = getattr(settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW\", 3600)\n\n        # Get client IP address\n        client_ip = request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"unknown\")\n\n        # Create cache key for this IP\n        cache_key = f\"rate_limit:{client_ip}\"\n\n        # Get current count from cache\n        request_count = cache.get(cache_key, 0)\n\n        # Increment the count\n        request_count += 1\n\n        # Check if limit exceeded\n        if request_count > rate_limit_requests:\n            return HttpResponseTooManyRequests()\n\n        # Update cache with new count\n        cache.set(cache_key, request_count, rate_limit_window)\n\n        # Allow the request to continue\n        return None\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":360,"cache_read_input_tokens":75255,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":360},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3e7f468f-524d-4a77-9857-9c3e625f3add","uuid":"5a67141b-dcf3-4f71-a113-cd5456827802"}
